'''Write a python function to remove odd numbers from a given list.'''
def odd_numbers(input_list):
    '''Return a new list of only the odd numbers in the input list.'''
    new_list = []
    for i in input_list:
        if i % 2!=0:
            new_list.append(i)
    return new_list

'''Write a python function to remove odd numbers from a given list.'''
def odd_numbers(input_list):
    '''Return a new list of only the odd numbers in the input list.'''
    new_list = []
    for i in input_list:
        if i % 2!=0:
            new_list.append(i)
    return new_list

def odd_numbers(input_list):
    '''Return a new list of only the odd numbers in the input list.'''
    new_list = []
    for i in input_list:
        if i % 2!=0:
            new_list.append(i)
    return new_list

'''Write a python function to remove odd numbers from a given list.'''
def odd_numbers(input_list):
    '''Return a new list of only the odd numbers in the input list.'''
    new_list = []
    for i in input_list:
        if i % 2!=0:
            new_list.append(i)

'''Write a python function to remove odd numbers from a given list.'''
def odd_numbers(input_list):
    '''Return a new list of only the odd numbers in the input list.'''
    new_list = []
    for i in input_list:
        if i % 2!=0:
            new_list.append(i)
    return new_list
